    display: inline;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





Please provide a brief explanation of the security issue.



<b class="line"><!---->Please provide a brief explanation of the security issue.<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





While encoding lossy webp with alpha, trials will be performed with different filtering settings to find the option that compresses the alpha data the best. If a certain stage during the alpha encode fails to allocate memory, the buffer used for a trial encode will be freed [1]. During that failed attempt the trail buffer was not reinitialized and refers to an earlier, successful run. The pointer may have been cached in another variable [2] which will be freed on receipt of the error [3].



<span class="line"><!---->While encoding lossy webp with alpha, trials will be performed with different filtering settings to find the option that compresses the alpha data the best. If a certain stage during the alpha encode fails to allocate memory, the buffer used for a trial encode will be freed [1]. During that failed attempt the trail buffer was not reinitialized and refers to an earlier, successful run. The pointer may have been cached in another variable [2] which will be freed on receipt of the error [3].<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





See also: 



<span class="line"><!---->See also: <!----></span>





https://crbug.com/webp/603



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crbug.com/webp/603"><!---->https://crbug.com/webp/603<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#260



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#260"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#260<!----></a>



<br>





[2] 



<span class="line"><!---->[2] <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#258



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#258"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#258<!----></a>



<br>





[3] 



<span class="line"><!---->[3] <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#287



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#287"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/webm/libwebp/+/refs/tags/v1.3.0/src/enc/alpha_enc.c#287<!----></a>



<br>

VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 110.0.5481.177 stable + beta, dev and tip of tree



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 110.0.5481.177 stable + beta, dev and tip of tree<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: All



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: All<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





This requires an OOM condition for a specific allocation to fail while encoding RGBA. This should be reproducible with <canvas>, but given the need for OOM there isn't a reliable reproduction in Chrome. It may be more likely to happen with a large canvas and a 32-bit build.



<span class="line"><!---->This requires an OOM condition for a specific allocation to fail while encoding RGBA. This should be reproducible with &lt;canvas&gt;, but given the need for OOM there isn't a reliable reproduction in Chrome. It may be more likely to happen with a large canvas and a 32-bit build.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>

<b class="line"><!---->FOR CRASHES, PLEASE INCLUDE THE FOLLOWING ADDITIONAL INFORMATION<!----></b>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->Type of crash: tab<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Crash State: N/A<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Client ID (if relevant): N/A<!----></span>

<b class="line"><!---->Externally reported security bugs may appear in Chrome release notes. If<!----></b>

<b class="line"><!---->this bug is included, how would you like to be credited?<!----></b>

Hello,



<span class="line"><!---->Hello,<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Google Open Source Software Vulnerability Reward Program panel has decided to issue a reward of $1337 for your report. Congratulations!



<span class="line"><!---->Google Open Source Software Vulnerability Reward Program panel has decided to issue a reward of $1337 for your report. Congratulations!<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Rationale for this decision:



<span class="line"><!---->Rationale for this decision:<!----></span>



<br>





Target is in "Standard OSS projects" tier.



<span class="line"><!---->Target is in "Standard OSS projects" tier.<!----></span>



<br>





Issue category is "Product vulnerabilities".



<span class="line"><!---->Issue category is "Product vulnerabilities".<!----></span>



<br>





We applied 1 downgrade from the base amount, since the exploitation requires an OOM condition.



<span class="line"><!---->We applied 1 downgrade from the base amount, since the exploitation requires an OOM condition.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;

          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);

          position: absolute;

 <script type="text/javascript" nonce="">
 window.addEventListener('load', () => {
 window.getTSMonClient().recordIssueDetailSpaTiming();
 });
 </script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="">
 runOnLoad(function() {
 if (typeof(ClientLogger) === "function") {
 let cl = new ClientLogger("issues");
 if (cl.started("new-issue")) {
 cl.logEnd("new-issue", null, 120 * 1000);
 }
 if (cl.started("issue-search")) {
 cl.logEnd("issue-search");
 }
 }
 });
</script>
